     1	"use strict";
     2	
     3	var htmlparser = require("htmlparser2"),
     4	  md = require("@textlint/markdown-to-ast");
     5	
     6	function addLinenos(lines, headers) {
     7	  var current = 0, line;
     8	
     9	  return headers.map(function (x) {
    10	    for (var lineno = current; lineno < lines.length; lineno++) {
    11	      line = lines[lineno];
    12	      if (new RegExp(x.text[0]).test(line)) {
    13	        current = lineno;
    14	        x.line = lineno;
    15	        x.name = x.text.join("");
    16	        return x;
    17	      }
    18	    }
    19	
    20	    // in case we didn't find a matching line, which is odd,
    21	    // we'll have to assume it's right on the next line
    22	    x.line = ++current;
    23	    x.name = x.text.join("");
    24	    return x;
    25	  });
    26	}
    27	
    28	function rankify(headers, max, min) {
    29	  return headers
    30	    .map(function (x) {
    31	      x.rank = parseInt(x.tag.slice(1), 10);
    32	      return x;
    33	    })
    34	    .filter(function (x) {
    35	      return x.rank <= max && x.rank >= min;
    36	    });
    37	}
    38	
    39	var go = (module.exports = function (lines, maxHeaderLevel, minHeaderLevel) {
    40	  var source = md
    41	    .parse(lines.join("\n"))
    42	    .children.filter(function (node) {
    43	      return node.type === md.Syntax.HtmlBlock || node.type === md.Syntax.Html;
    44	    })
    45	    .map(function (node) {
    46	      return node.raw;
    47	    })
    48	    .join("\n");
    49	
    50	  //var headers = [], grabbing = null, text = [];
    51	  var headers = [],
    52	    grabbing = [],
    53	    text = [];
    54	
    55	  var parser = new htmlparser.Parser(
    56	    {
    57	      onopentag: function (name, attr) {
    58	        // Short circuit if we're already inside a pre
    59	        if (grabbing[grabbing.length - 1] === "pre") return;
    60	
    61	        if (name === "pre" || /h\d/.test(name)) {
    62	          grabbing.push(name);
    63	        }
    64	      },
    65	      ontext: function (text_) {
    66	        // Explicitly skip pre tags, and implicitly skip all others
    67	        if (grabbing.length === 0 || grabbing[grabbing.length - 1] === "pre")
    68	          return;
    69	
    70	        text.push(text_);
    71	      },
    72	      onclosetag: function (name) {
    73	        if (grabbing.length === 0) return;
    74	        if (grabbing[grabbing.length - 1] === name) {
    75	          var tag = grabbing.pop();
    76	          headers.push({ text: text, tag: tag });
    77	          text = [];
    78	        }
    79	      },
    80	    },
    81	    { decodeEntities: true },
    82	  );
    83	
    84	  parser.write(source);
    85	  parser.end();

    87	  headers = addLinenos(lines, headers);
    88	  // consider anything past h4 to small to warrant a link, may be made configurable in the future
    89	  headers = rankify(headers, maxHeaderLevel, minHeaderLevel);
    90	  return headers;
    91	});

var htmlparser = require('htmlparser2');
var md = require('@textlint/markdown-to-ast');

// Simulate what happens with a problematic HTML content
var source = '<p>text</p>';
var grabbing = [];
var text = [];
var headers = [];

var parser = new htmlparser.Parser({
  onopentag: function(name, attr) {
    if (grabbing[grabbing.length - 1] === 'pre') return;
    if (name === 'pre' || /h\d/.test(name)) {
      grabbing.push(name);
    }
  },
  ontext: function(text_) {
    if (grabbing.length === 0 || grabbing[grabbing.length - 1] === 'pre') return;
    text.push(text_);
  },
  onclosetag: function(name) {
    if (grabbing.length === 0) return;
    if (grabbing[grabbing.length - 1] === name) {
      var tag = grabbing.pop();
      headers.push({ text: text, tag: tag });
      text = [];
    }
  }
}, { decodeEntities: true });

parser.write('<p>text</p>');
parser.end();
console.log('Headers:', JSON.stringify(headers));

     3	var anchor = require("anchor-markdown-header"),
     4	  updateSection = require("update-section"),
     5	  getHtmlHeaders = require("./get-html-headers"),
     6	  md = require("@textlint/markdown-to-ast");
     7	
     8	var commentTypes = {
     9	  md: {
    10	    start: "<!--",
    11	    end: "-->",
    12	    escapedStart: "<!--",
    13	  },
    14	  mdx: {
    15	    start: "{/*",
    16	    end: "*/}",
    17	    escapedStart: "{\/\\*",
    18	  }
    19	}
    20	
    21	var { start: startMd , end: endMd } = generateComments('md')
    22	
    23	function matchesStart(syntax) {
    24	  var commentEscapedStart = commentTypes[syntax].escapedStart
    25	  return function(line){
    26	    return new RegExp(`${commentEscapedStart} START doctoc `).test(line);
    27	  }
    28	}
    29	
    30	function matchesEnd(syntax) {
    31	  var commentEscapedStart = commentTypes[syntax].escapedStart
    32	  return function(line){
    33	    return new RegExp(`${commentEscapedStart} END doctoc `).test(line);
    34	  }
    35	}
    36	
    37	function notNull(x) { return  x !== null; }
    38	
    39	function addAnchor(mode, header) {
    40	  header.anchor = anchor(header.name, mode, header.instance);
    41	  return header;
    42	}
    43	
    44	function isString(y) {
    45	  return typeof y === 'string';
    46	}
    47	
    48	function generateComments(syntax){
    49	  var commentStart = commentTypes[syntax].start
    50	  , commentEnd = commentTypes[syntax].end;
    51	
    52	  var start = `${commentStart} START doctoc generated TOC please keep comment here to allow auto update ${commentEnd}\n` +
    53	            `${commentStart} DON\'T EDIT THIS SECTION, INSTEAD RE-RUN doctoc TO UPDATE ${commentEnd}`
    54	  , end   = `${commentStart} END doctoc generated TOC please keep comment here to allow auto update ${commentEnd}`
    55	  , skipTag = `${commentStart} DOCTOC SKIP ${commentEnd}\n`;
    56	
    57	  exports.start = start;
    58	  exports.end = end;
    59	  return { start, end, skipTag}
    60	}
    61	
    62	function getMarkdownHeaders (lines, maxHeaderLevel, minHeaderLevel) {
    63	  function extractText (header) {
    64	    return header.children
    65	      .map(function (x) {
    66	        if (x.type === md.Syntax.Link) {
    67	          return extractText(x);
    68	        }
    69	        else if (x.type === md.Syntax.Image) {
    70	          // Images (at least on GitHub, untested elsewhere) are given a hyphen
    71	          // in the slug. We can achieve this behavior by adding an '*' to the
    72	          // TOC entry. Think of it as a "magic char" that represents the image.
    73	          return '*';
    74	        }
    75	        else {
    76	          return x.raw;
    77	        }
    78	      })
    79	      .join("");
    80	  }
    81	
    82	  return md
    83	    .parse(lines.join("\n"))
    84	    .children.filter(function (x) {
    85	      return x.type === md.Syntax.Header;
    86	    })
    87	    .map(function (x) {
    88	      return x.depth >= minHeaderLevel && (!maxHeaderLevel || x.depth <= maxHeaderLevel)
    89	        ? { rank :  x.depth
    90	          , name :  extractText(x)
    91	          , line :  x.loc.start.line
    92	          }
    93	        : null;
    94	    })
    95	    .filter(notNull);
    96	}
    97	
    98	function countHeaders(headers, mode) {
    99	  var instances = {};
   100	
   101	  for (var i = 0; i < headers.length; i++) {
   102	    var header = headers[i];
   103	    var name = anchor(header.name, mode).split('#')[1].slice(0, -1);
   104	
   105	    if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(instances, name)) {
   106	      // `instances.hasOwnProperty(name)` fails when there’s an instance named "hasOwnProperty".
   107	      instances[name]++;
   108	    } else {
   109	      instances[name] = 0;
   110	    }
   111	
   112	    header.instance = instances[name];
   113	    header.tag = name;
   114	  }
   115	
   116	  return headers;
   117	}
   118	
   119	function getLinesToToc(lines, currentToc, info, processAll) {
   120	  if (processAll || !currentToc) return lines;
   121	
   122	  var tocableStart = 0;
   123	
   124	  // when updating an existing toc, we only take the headers into account
   125	  // that are below the existing toc
   126	  if (info.hasEnd) tocableStart = info.endIdx + 1;
   127	
   128	  return lines.slice(tocableStart);
   129	}
   130	
   131	// Use document context as well as command line args to infer the title
   132	function determineTitle(title, notitle, lines, info) {
   133	  var defaultTitle = '**Table of Contents**  *generated with [DocToc](https://github.com/thlorenz/doctoc)*';
   134	
   135	  if (notitle) return "";
   136	  if (title) return title;
   137	  return info.hasStart ? lines[info.startIdx + 2] : defaultTitle;
   138	}
   139	
   140	exports = module.exports = function transform(content, mode, maxHeaderLevel, minHeaderLevel, minTocItems, title, notitle, entryPrefix, processAll, updateOnly, syntax, padTitle) {
   141	  syntax = syntax || "md"
   142	  var { skipTag, start, end } = generateComments(syntax)
   143	  var matchesStartBySyntax = matchesStart(syntax)
   144	  var matchesEndBySyntax = matchesEnd(syntax)
   145	  var index = content.indexOf(skipTag);
   146	  if (index === 0 || (index >= 0 && content[index-1] === '\n')) return { transformed: false };
   147	
   148	  mode = mode || "github.com";
   149	  entryPrefix = entryPrefix || "-";
   150	  minHeaderLevel = minHeaderLevel || 1;
   151	
   152	  if (isNaN(minTocItems) || minTocItems < 1){
   153	    minTocItems = 1;
   154	  }
   155	
   156	  if (padTitle === undefined){
   157	    padTitle = notitle || false;
   158	  }
   159	
   160	  // only limit *HTML* headings by default
   161	  var maxHeaderLevelHtml = maxHeaderLevel || 4;
   162	
   163	  var lines = content.split('\n')
   164	    , info = updateSection.parse(lines, matchesStartBySyntax, matchesEndBySyntax)
   165	
   166	  if (!info.hasStart && updateOnly) {
   167	    return { transformed: false };
   168	  }
   169	
   170	  var inferredTitle = determineTitle(title, notitle, lines, info);
   171	
   172	  var titleSeparator = inferredTitle ? '\n\n' : '\n';
   173	  var titlePadding = padTitle && inferredTitle ? '\n' : '';
   174	
   175	  var currentToc = info.hasStart && lines.slice(info.startIdx, info.endIdx + 1).join('\n')
   176	    , linesToToc = getLinesToToc(lines, currentToc, info, processAll);
   177	
   178	  var headers = getMarkdownHeaders(linesToToc, maxHeaderLevel, minHeaderLevel)
   179	    .concat(getHtmlHeaders(linesToToc, maxHeaderLevelHtml, minHeaderLevel))
   180	
   181	  headers.sort(function (a, b) {
   182	    return a.line - b.line;
   183	  });
   184	
   185	  var allHeaders = countHeaders(headers, mode),
   186	    lowestRank = allHeaders.reduce((min, h) => Math.min(min, h.rank), Infinity),
   187	    linkedHeaders = allHeaders.map(h => addAnchor(mode, h));
   188	
   189	  // 4 spaces required for proper indention on Bitbucket and GitLab
   190	  var indentation = (mode === 'bitbucket.org' || mode === 'gitlab.com') ? '    ' : '  ';
   191	
   192	  var toc = '';
   193	  var wrappedToc;
   194	
   195	  if (linkedHeaders.length >= minTocItems) {
   196	    toc = 
   197	      titlePadding
   198	    + inferredTitle
   199	    + titleSeparator
   200	    + linkedHeaders
   201	        .map(function (x) {
   202	          return indentation.repeat(x.rank - lowestRank) + entryPrefix + ' ' + x.anchor;
   203	        })
   204	        .join('\n')
   205	    + '\n';
   206	    wrappedToc = start + '\n' + toc + '\n' + end;
   207	  }
   208	  else {
   209	    wrappedToc =  start + '\n' + end;
   210	  }
   211	
   212	  var data;
   213	  if (currentToc != wrappedToc){
   214	    data = updateSection(lines.join('\n'), wrappedToc, matchesStartBySyntax, matchesEndBySyntax, true);
   215	  }
   216	  return { transformed : currentToc != wrappedToc, data : data, toc: toc, wrappedToc: wrappedToc };
   217	};
   218	
   219	exports.start = startMd;
   220	exports.end = endMd;

2026-05-30 15:19:59,349 - INFO - swea-agent-thlorenz__doctoc-328 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now I understand the full picture. The `addLinenos` function in `get-html-headers.js` tries to match the HTML header text against each line using a regular expression. But the text might contain special regex characters.

The simplest and most correct fix is to escape the regex special characters in `x.text[0]` before passing it to `new RegExp()`. Alternatively, we could use `line.indexOf(x.text[0]) !== -1` which would be simpler and avoid regex entirely.

Let me think about which approach is better. Using `indexOf` would be simpler and avoid the regex escaping issue entirely. But using regex might be needed for some flexibility in matching. However, looking at the code, it seems like the intent is just to find which line contains the header text. A simple string match should work.

But wait, let me check: could there be cases where the text has different whitespace or formatting? The regex `new RegExp(x.text[0]).test(line)` would match the text anywhere in the line. `indexOf` would do the same. So switching to `indexOf` should be safe.

However, to be more conservative, I could also just escape the regex. Let me check if there's already a utility for escaping regex in the codebase:

function addLinenos(lines, headers) {
  var current = 0, line;

  return headers.map(function (x) {
    for (var lineno = current; lineno < lines.length; lineno++) {
      line = lines[lineno];
      if (new RegExp(escapeRegExp(x.text[0])).test(line)) {
        current = lineno;
        x.line = lineno;
        x.name = x.text.join("");

    x.line = ++current;
    x.name = x.text.join("");
    return x;
  });

var getHtmlHeaders = require('./lib/get-html-headers.js');

// Test 1: The original error case from PR
// This uses backtick characters that when combined with forward slash
// create an invalid regex
var textWithBackticks = '` element tells the rendering program that the content inside is a form.\n\nThe end tag is just like the start tag except that it has a forward slash added just after the less-than sign (`';

function escapeRegExp(string) {
  return string.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\\/]/g, '\\$&');
}

  var re = new RegExp(escapeRegExp(textWithBackticks));
  console.log('Test 1 PASS: Regex created successfully');
} catch (e) {
  console.log('Test 1 FAIL:', e.message);
}

Now I see - the test has HTML tags like `<h2>not me code</h2>` inside `<code>` tags. The `htmlparser2` parser should ignore these because `<code>` is not `pre` or an `h*` tag. But wait, looking at the code, only `pre` and `h\d` tags are tracked. So `<code>` tags would be ignored and `h2` inside would be grabbed. Let me trace through the logic more carefully.

Actually, looking at the code in `get-html-headers.js`:

```javascript
onopentag: function (name, attr) {
    // Short circuit if we're already inside a pre
    if (grabbing[grabbing.length - 1] === "pre") return;

    if (name === "pre" || /h\d/.test(name)) {
        grabbing.push(name);
    }
},
```

So it only pushes `pre` or `h\d` tags. But `<code>` is not pushed, so `<h2>` inside `<code>` would still be pushed. That seems like a separate issue though.

The key issue right now is that my `escapeRegExp` function fails when `x.text[0]` is `undefined`. Let me look at when that could happen. The `htmlparser2` might produce headers with empty text arrays. Let me check:






🎬 ACTION
cd /testbed && node -e "
var htmlparser = require('htmlparser2');

var source = '<h2>not me code</h2>';
var grabbing = [];
var text = [];
var headers = [];

var parser = new htmlparser.Parser({
  onopentag: function(name, attr) {
    if (grabbing[grabbing.length - 1] === 'pre') return;
    if (name === 'pre' || /h\d/.test(name)) {
      grabbing.push(name);
    }
  },
  ontext: function(text_) {
    if (grabbing.length === 0 || grabbing[grabbing.length - 1] === 'pre') return;
    text.push(text_);
  },
  onclosetag: function(name) {
    if (grabbing.length === 0) return;
    if (grabbing[grabbing.length - 1] === name) {
      var tag = grabbing.pop();
      headers.push({ text: text, tag: tag });
      text = [];
    }
  }
}, { decodeEntities: true });

// Parse the code tag scenario
parser.write('<code><h2>not me code</h2></code>');
parser.end();
console.log('Headers:', JSON.stringify(headers));

     1	"use strict";
     2	
     3	var htmlparser = require("htmlparser2"),
     4	  md = require("@textlint/markdown-to-ast");
     5	
     6	function escapeRegExp(string) {
     7	  if (string == null) return "";
     8	  return string.toString().replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\\/]/g, "\\$&");
     9	}
    10	
    11	function addLinenos(lines, headers) {
    12	  var current = 0, line;
    13	
    14	  return headers.map(function (x) {
    15	    for (var lineno = current; lineno < lines.length; lineno++) {
    16	      line = lines[lineno];
    17	      if (new RegExp(escapeRegExp(x.text[0])).test(line)) {
    18	        current = lineno;
    19	        x.line = lineno;
    20	        x.name = x.text.join("");
    21	        return x;
    22	      }
    23	    }
    24	
    25	    // in case we didn't find a matching line, which is odd,
    26	    // we'll have to assume it's right on the next line
    27	    x.line = ++current;
    28	    x.name = x.text.join("");
    29	    return x;
    30	  });
    31	}
    32	
    33	function rankify(headers, max, min) {
    34	  return headers
    35	    .map(function (x) {
    36	      x.rank = parseInt(x.tag.slice(1), 10);
    37	      return x;
    38	    })
    39	    .filter(function (x) {
    40	      return x.rank <= max && x.rank >= min;
    41	    });
    42	}
    43	
    44	var go = (module.exports = function (lines, maxHeaderLevel, minHeaderLevel) {
    45	  var source = md
    46	    .parse(lines.join("\n"))
    47	    .children.filter(function (node) {
    48	      return node.type === md.Syntax.HtmlBlock || node.type === md.Syntax.Html;
    49	    })
    50	    .map(function (node) {
    51	      return node.raw;
    52	    })
    53	    .join("\n");
    54	
    55	  //var headers = [], grabbing = null, text = [];
    56	  var headers = [],
    57	    grabbing = [],
    58	    text = [];
    59	
    60	  var parser = new htmlparser.Parser(
    61	    {
    62	      onopentag: function (name, attr) {
    63	        // Short circuit if we're already inside a pre
    64	        if (grabbing[grabbing.length - 1] === "pre") return;
    65	
    66	        if (name === "pre" || /h\d/.test(name)) {
    67	          grabbing.push(name);
    68	        }
    69	      },
    70	      ontext: function (text_) {
    71	        // Explicitly skip pre tags, and implicitly skip all others
    72	        if (grabbing.length === 0 || grabbing[grabbing.length - 1] === "pre")
    73	          return;
    74	
    75	        text.push(text_);
    76	      },
    77	      onclosetag: function (name) {
    78	        if (grabbing.length === 0) return;
    79	        if (grabbing[grabbing.length - 1] === name) {
    80	          var tag = grabbing.pop();
    81	          headers.push({ text: text, tag: tag });
    82	          text = [];
    83	        }
    84	      },
    85	    },
    86	    { decodeEntities: true },
    87	  );
    88	
    89	  parser.write(source);
    90	  parser.end();
    91	
    92	  headers = addLinenos(lines, headers);
    93	  // consider anything past h4 to small to warrant a link, may be made configurable in the future
    94	  headers = rankify(headers, maxHeaderLevel, minHeaderLevel);
    95	  return headers;
    96	});
